# Controversial Questions to Prof.Jonathan Brown and Dr. Shadee ElMasri (MH Podcast #6) (2020-07-06)

![alt Controversial Questions to Prof.Jonathan Brown and Dr. Shadee ElMasri (MH Podcast #6)](7jXye1-Wbug.jpg "Controversial Questions to Prof.Jonathan Brown and Dr. Shadee ElMasri (MH Podcast #6)")

## Description

Here Prof.Jonathan Brown, Dr. Shadee Masri and I discuss certain issues that people may have against what they may have written/said. They clarify and give context to their views. 
Issues range from LGBTQ, Yaqeen institute, statements regarding the Prophet (s.a.w) etc. 

Twitter: https://twitter.com/mohammed_hijab?s=20
Instagram: https://www.instagram.com/mohammedhijabofficial/?hl=en
Facebook: https://www.facebook.com/brothermohammedhijab/
Soundcloud: https://soundcloud.com/mohammed-hijab-465985305

21:00 We shouldn’t support others just because they can help Muslims (no quid pro quo)

32:00 Prophetic model is neither a right model or a left model
41:00 Soft-Liberalism/(Ottoman) Millet system thought experiment

1:19:50 MH suggestions to JB to avoid shubha
